Once upon a time, there was a girl named jessie. Her (slightly) ginger hair and perfect face were the most beautiful anyone had ever seen. But Jessie has a problem. she was far too good for the fairy tale land she lived in. All the other girls were simply too jealous of her perfection. So Jessie decided to go out into the world and find where she could truly belong. Fist she traveled far, far away into a strange and new world called "psych." Here jessie met a stranger named Morgan who told her the wonder of pineapples and obscure references. And thus jessie and morgan decided to continue their journey. Next they traveled to a distant place called "Water Polo Town" where people loved to play and work out all day! It was odd, but jessie decided she LOVED it. So she and morgan stayed for a while, and in no time they met a new friend called Paige. The three became best friends and decided it was time to look for their own town. In this search they met a girl named Tori, and Tori showed them how to get others to join their town! But soon, the four decided to move on and in the next town, called "Academically obsessed," they met another friend. Her name was Kayla and soon she loved Jessie the most of them all. And so the best friendship ever was formed. Though Jessie never could find anyone more beautiful than her! And they lived happily ever after. Love, Kayla
